#!/usr/bin/env python3

"""
prayer_log_monitor.py
Chronos CoreAlpha PoC ãƒ¢ã‚¸ãƒ¥ãƒ¼ãƒ«
ç¥ˆã‚Šï¼ˆæ„å›³ï¼‰ãƒ­ã‚°ã‚’ç›£è¦–ã—ã¦è¨˜éŒ²ã™ã‚‹ã€‚
"""

import datetime
import os

LOG_DIR = "/var/log/chronos"
LOG_FILE = os.path.join(LOG_DIR, "prayer_log.txt")

def ensure_log_dir():
    os.makedirs(LOG_DIR, exist_ok=True)

def log_prayer(message: str):
    ensure_log_dir()
    with open(LOG_FILE, "a") as f:
        timestamp = datetime.datetime.now().isoformat()
        f.write(f"[{timestamp}] PRAYER: {message}\n")

def main():
    # ä»®ã®æ„å›³ãƒ­ã‚°ï¼ˆå¾Œã§å®Ÿéš›ã®VPSã‚³ãƒãƒ³ãƒ‰ã‚„APIã‹ã‚‰å–å¾—ã«ç½®ãæ›ãˆï¼‰
    dummy_intent = "ãƒ¦ãƒ¼ã‚¶ãƒ¼ã‹ã‚‰ã®æ„å›³ã‚³ãƒãƒ³ãƒ‰"
    log_prayer(dummy_intent)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

        print("ãƒ­ã‚°ãŒã¾ã å­˜åœ¨ã—ã¾ã›ã‚“ã€‚")

#!/usr/bin/env python3
# ---
# type: module
# version: v1.0.0
# updated: 2025-07-16T00:00:00+09:00
# title: prayer_log_monitor.py
# namespace: nancy.chronos.alpha
# category: PoCãƒ¢ã‚¸ãƒ¥ãƒ¼ãƒ«
# status: active
# thread_id: thread_Nancy_X_20250716_00000060
# linked_modules:
#   - nancy/chronos/alpha/feedback_anomaly_detector.py
# description: >
#   VPSä¸Šã®æ„å›³ãƒ­ã‚°ã‚’ç›£è¦–ã—ã¦è¨˜éŒ²ã™ã‚‹PoCãƒ¢ã‚¸ãƒ¥ãƒ¼ãƒ«ã€‚
# ---

"""
prayer_log_monitor.py
Chronos CoreAlpha PoC ãƒ¢ã‚¸ãƒ¥ãƒ¼ãƒ«
ç¥ˆã‚Šï¼ˆæ„å›³ï¼‰ãƒ­ã‚°ã‚’ç›£è¦–ã—ã¦è¨˜éŒ²ã™ã‚‹ã€‚
"""

import datetime
import os #

LOG_DIR = os.path.expanduser("~/logs/chronos")
LOG_FILE = os.path.join(LOG_DIR, "prayer_log.txt")

def ensure_log_dir():
    os.makedirs(LOG_DIR, exist_ok=True)

def log_prayer(message: str):
    ensure_log_dir()
    with open(LOG_FILE, "a") as f:
        timestamp = datetime.datetime.now().isoformat()
        f.write(f"[{timestamp}] PRAYER: {message}\n")

def main():
    dummy_intent = "ãƒ¦ãƒ¼ã‚¶ãƒ¼ã‹ã‚‰ã®æ„å›³ã‚³ãƒãƒ³ãƒ‰"
    log_prayer(dummy_intent)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

def main():
    detect_anomalies()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
# ---
# type: module
# version: v1.0.0
# updated: 2025-07-16T00:00:00+09:00
# title: prayer_log_monitor.py
# namespace: nancy.chronos.alpha
# category: PoCãƒ¢ã‚¸ãƒ¥ãƒ¼ãƒ«
# status: active
# thread_id: thread_Nancy_X_20250716_00000060
# linked_modules:
#   - nancy/chronos/alpha/feedback_anomaly_detector.py
# description: >
#   VPSä¸Šã®æ„å›³ãƒ­ã‚°ã‚’ç›£è¦–ã—ã¦è¨˜éŒ²ã™ã‚‹PoCãƒ¢ã‚¸ãƒ¥ãƒ¼ãƒ«ã€‚

"""
prayer_log_monitor.py
Chronos CoreAlpha PoC ãƒ¢ã‚¸ãƒ¥ãƒ¼ãƒ«
ç¥ˆã‚Šï¼ˆæ„å›³ï¼‰ãƒ­ã‚°ã‚’ç›£è¦–ã—ã¦è¨˜éŒ²ã™ã‚‹ã€‚
"""

import datetime
import os

LOG_DIR = os.path.expanduser("~/logs/chronos")
LOG_FILE = os.path.join(LOG_DIR, "prayer_log.txt")

def ensure_log_dir():
    os.makedirs(LOG_DIR, exist_ok=True)

def log_prayer(message: str):
    ensure_log_dir()
    with open(LOG_FILE, "a") as f:
        timestamp = datetime.datetime.now().isoformat()
        f.write(f"[{timestamp}] PRAYER: {message}\n")

def main():
    dummy_intent = "ãƒ¦ãƒ¼ã‚¶ãƒ¼ã‹ã‚‰ã®æ„å›³ã‚³ãƒãƒ³ãƒ‰"
    log_prayer(dummy_intent)

    main()

# 
# Each task to run has to be defined through a single line
# indicating with different fields when the task will be run
# and what command to run for the task
# 
# To define the time you can provide concrete values for
# minute (m), hour (h), day of month (dom), month (mon),
# and day of week (dow) or use '*' in these fields (for 'any').
# 
# Notice that tasks will be started based on the cron's system
# daemon's notion of time and timezones.
# 
# Output of the crontab jobs (including errors) is sent through
# email to the user the crontab file belongs to (unless redirected).
# 
# For example, you can run a backup of all your user accounts
# at 5 a.m every week with:
# 0 5 * * 1 tar -zcf /var/backups/home.tgz /home/
# 
# For more information see the manual pages of crontab(5) and cron(8)
# 
# m h  dom mon dow   command

"""
command_log_monitor.py
Chronos CoreAlpha PoC ãƒ¢ã‚¸ãƒ¥ãƒ¼ãƒ«
ã‚³ãƒãƒ³ãƒ‰å±¥æ­´ãƒ­ã‚°ã‚’ç›£è¦–ã—ã¦è¨˜éŒ²ã™ã‚‹ã€‚
"""

import datetime
import os

LOG_DIR = os.path.expanduser("~/logs/chronos")
LOG_FILE = os.path.join(LOG_DIR, "command_log.txt")

def ensure_log_dir():
    os.makedirs(LOG_DIR, exist_ok=True)

def log_command(message: str):
    ensure_log_dir()
    with open(LOG_FILE, "a") as f:
        timestamp = datetime.datetime.now().isoformat()
        f.write(f"[{timestamp}] COMMAND: {message}\n")

def main():
    dummy_command = "ãƒ¦ãƒ¼ã‚¶ãƒ¼ã‹ã‚‰ã®æ„å›³ã‚³ãƒãƒ³ãƒ‰"
    log_command(dummy_command)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

# Edit this file to introduce tasks to be run by cron.
# 
# Each task to run has to be defined through a single line
# indicating with different fields when the task will be run
# and what command to run for the task
# 
# To define the time you can provide concrete values for
# minute (m), hour (h), day of month (dom), month (mon),
# and day of week (dow) or use '*' in these fields (for 'any').
# 
# Notice that tasks will be started based on the cron's system
# daemon's notion of time and timezones.
# 
# Output of the crontab jobs (including errors) is sent through
# email to the user the crontab file belongs to (unless redirected).

# at 5 a.m every week with:
# 0 5 * * 1 tar -zcf /var/backups/home.tgz /home/
